id=protocolNotFound.longDesc
en=The address (URL) starts with a protocol that is not recognized by the browser. A protocol is the part at the front of the address, such as http: or ftp: which tells the browser how to connect to the site. In this instance, the protocol is unknown so loading cannot continue. Check that the address is correct before retrying.
tr=無法辨視網址(URL)使用的通訊協定。通訊協定指的是網址開頭的部份，如「http:」或「ftp:」。請確定網址正確無誤。

tr=錯誤：連線失敗

id=connectionFailure.longDesc
en=The browser was unable to connect to the specified site, even though it exists. This may be because the site does not accept connections from your computer, the service may be down, or the site does not support the service or port that you tried to connect to.
tr=指定網站的電腦有開機，但瀏覽器無法連線：可能是網站拒絕你的連線要求、它停止服務，或 Port 不對。

id=netTimeout.title
en=Net Timeout Error
tr=網路逾時錯誤

id=netTimeout.longDesc
en=The browser timed out while trying to connect to the specified site. The site may be experiencing high loads that are slowing it down, or network problems are preventing data from being received from it in a timely manner. If the site is likely to be busy, consider waiting a few moments before retrying the request.
tr=瀏覽器試圖連線至指定網站時逾時。網站可能目前流量太大無法連線或網路有問題。你可以稍後再試試看。

id=redirectLoop.title
en=Redirect Loop Error
tr=重新導向(Redirect)發生迴圈錯誤

id=redirectLoop.longDesc
en=The browser has stopped a connection because the site is redirecting requests to itself in a manner which prevents it from ever completing.
tr=瀏覽器停止連線，因為此網站一直在重復無止盡的重新指向(Redirect)。

id=unknownSocketType.title
en=Unknown Socket Error
tr=未知的Socket錯誤

id=unknownSocketType.longDesc
en=The site responded to the network request in an unexpected manner. This may be due to address (URL) using the wrong protocol for the specified port, or a non-standard configuration on the site which is running different services than expected.
tr=伺服器回應方式錯誤。可能是你的網址 (URL) 通訊協定錯誤，或是指定了錯誤的 Port。

id=netReset.title
en=Net Reset Error
tr=網路重設錯誤

id=generic.longDesc
en=The page could not be loaded, possibly because it does not exist or the location is incorrect.<br/>Check that the address (URL) is valid and correctly formatted.
tr=頁面無法載入，可能是網頁不存在或網址錯誤。<br/>;請檢查網址(URL)是否正確。

id=netReset.longDesc
en=The link to the site was dropped unexpectedly while negotiating a connection or transferring data. This may be due to a network fault somewhere between the site and your computer. If the problem persists, consult your system documentation, administrator or Internet Service Provider (ISP) as appropriate for further assistance.
tr=與網站的連線不正常的中斷了。可能是中間的網路有問題。如果此問題持續發生，請檢查你的系統，或跟管理員及網路提供者（ISP）要求協助。

id=netOffline.title
en=Offline Error
tr=離線錯誤

id=netOffline.longDesc
en=The browser is currently offline and cannot connect to the requested site. Place your browser in online mode before trying again.
tr=瀏覽器離線中，無法連線到指定的網站。請切到連線模式後重試。

id=malformedURI.title
en=Invalid Address Error
tr=錯誤：不正確的網址

id=malformedURI.longDesc
en=The address (URL) is not a valid format and cannot be read. A typical address will start with &quot;http://&quot;, followed by an address, (e.g. www.netscape.com), followed by a path to the content (or just &quot;/&quot;). A common cause for the problem is using backslashes(\\) instead of forward slashes (/).
tr=網址(URL)格式不正確，無法讀入。標準的網址應該由「http://」開頭，接著一個位址（如www.mozilla.org），再接上一組路徑指向內容（或只有「/」）。 常見錯誤是用了倒斜線（\\）而非正確的斜線（/）。

id=fileNotFound.title
en=File Not Found Error
tr=錯誤：找不到檔案

id=fileNotFound.longDesc
en=The file specified by the address (URL) cannot be found. Check that the file exists and that you have sufficient permissions to view it.
tr=找不到由網址(URL)指定的檔案。請檢查檔案是否存在，你有沒有足夠的權限以檢視。

id=dnsNotFound.title
en=Address Not Found Error
tr=錯誤：找不到位址。

id=dnsNotFound.longDesc
en=The address (URL) does not correspond to a known site and could not be loaded. This could be due to a misspelling in the address or because the site does not exist. If the address is known to be valid, or if the problem occurs for many sites, it may be an issue with your proxy service (if you use one) or the directory name service lookup. In such cases you should consult your system documentation, administrator or Internet Service Provider (ISP) as appropriate for further assistance.
tr=無法辨視網址(URL)使用的通訊協定。通訊協定指的是網址開頭的部份，如「http:」或「ftp:」。請確定網址正確無誤。

id=protocolNotFound.title
en=Protocol Not Known Error
tr=錯誤：未知的通訊協定

tr=切換目前頻道的記錄(Log)功能。若<state>是|true|, |on|, |yes|, |1|則記錄， |false|, |off|, |no|, |0|則關閉。未給定<state>可顯示目前狀態。 狀態會被記住，所以開啟後若你關閉 Chatzilla 則下次連線時又會繼續記錄。

If <delete-pref> is provided and is |true|, |on|, |yes|, or |1|, or if <pref-name> starts with a minus ('-') character, then the preference will revert back to its default value.  If <network> is not provided, the current network is assumed.
